**Coste:** 4 | **Tipo:** Character | **Color:** Steel | **Tinta:** ‚úó | **Rareza:** Super Rare  
**Fuerza:** 3 | **Voluntad:** 5 | **Lore:** 1  
**Set:** Whispers in the Well (WHI #10) | [üñºÔ∏è Imagen](https://api.lorcana.ravensburger.com/images/en/set10/192_eb19530d334061f223ed0787de24d7097b23e7e8.jpg)


**Habilidades:**
- Boost 3 {i} (Once during your turn, you may pay 3 {i} to put
the top card of your deck facedown under this character.)
STUNNING TRANSFORMATION Whenever you put a card
under this character, you may banish chosen opposing
character. If you do, their player may reveal the top card
of their deck. If that card is a character or item card, they
may play it for free. Otherwise, they put it on the bottom of
their deck.
